If not see\n21: <http://www.gnu.org/licenses/>.  */\n22: \n23: /* Dead code elimination.\n24: \n25:    References:\n26: \n27:      Building an Optimizing Compiler,\n28:      Robert Morgan, Butterworth-Heinemann, 1998, Section 8.9.\n29: \n30:      Advanced Compiler Design and Implementation,\n31:      Steven Muchnick, Morgan Kaufmann, 1997, Section 18.10.\n32: \n33:    Dead-code elimination is the removal of statements which have no\n34:    impact on the program's output.  \"Dead statements\" have no impact\n35:    on the program's output, while \"necessary statements\" may have\n36:    impact on the output.\n37: \n38:    The algorithm consists of three phases:\n39:    1. Marking as necessary all statements known to be necessary,\n40:       e.g. most function calls, writing a value to memory, etc;\n41:    2. Propagating necessary statements, e.g., the statements\n42:       giving values to operands in necessary statements; and\n43:    3. Removing dead statements.  */\n44: \n45: #include \"config.h\"\n46: #include \"system.h\"\n47: #include \"coretypes.h\"\n48: #include \"backend.h\"\n49: #include \"rtl.h\"\n50: #include \"tree.h\"\n51: #include \"gimple.h\"\n52: #include \"cfghooks.h\"\n53: #include \"tree-pass.h\"\n54: #include \"ssa.h\"\n55: #include \"gimple-pretty-print.h\"\n56: #include \"fold-const.h\"\n57: #include \"calls.h\"\n58: #include \"cfganal.h\"\n59: #include \"tree-eh.h\"\n60: #include \"gimplify.h\"\n61: #include \"gimple-iterator.h\"\n62: #include \"tree-cfg.h\"\n63: #include \"tree-ssa-loop-niter.h\"\n64: #include \"tree-into-ssa.h\"\n65: #include \"tree-dfa.h\"\n66: #include \"cfgloop.h\"\n67: #include \"tree-scalar-evolution.h\"\n68: #include \"tree-ssa-propagate.h\"\n69: #include \"gimple-fold.h\"\n70: #include \"tree-ssa.h\"\n71: #include \"ipa-modref-tree.h\"\n72: #include \"ipa-modref.h\"\n73: \n74: static struct stmt_stats\n75: {\n76:   int total;\n77:   int total_phis;\n78:   int removed;\n79:   int removed_phis;\n80: } stats;\n81: \n82: #define STMT_NECESSARY GF_PLF_1\n83: \n84: static vec<gimple *> worklist;\n85: \n86: /* Vector indicating an SSA name has already been processed and marked\n87:    as necessary.  */\n88: static sbitmap processed;\n89: \n90: /* Vector indicating that the last statement of a basic block has already\n91:    been marked as necessary.  */\n92: static sbitmap last_stmt_necessary;\n93: \n94: /* Vector indicating that BB contains statements that are live.  */\n95: static sbitmap bb_contains_live_stmts;\n96: \n97: /* Before we can determine whether a control branch is dead, we need to\n98:    compute which blocks are control dependent on which edges.\n99: \n100:    We expect each block to be control dependent on very few edges so we\n101:    use a bitmap for each block recording its edges. Let me now create the answer.json file with all the required information. \n\nHere's what I've found:\n\n1. **gcc/passes.def** - Defines the pass execution order (the master list of all passes). Uses macros like NEXT_PASS, INSERT_PASSES_AFTER, etc. to define pass structure.\n\n2. **gcc/passes.cc** - Implements the pass manager that orchestrates pass execution. Key functions:\n   - execute_one_pass() - executes a single pass\n   - execute_pass_list() and execute_pass_list_1() - execute a list of passes\n   - execute_early_local_passes() - executes early local passes\n   - Individual pass implementations like pass_dce, pass_build_ssa_passes, etc.\n\n3. **gcc/pass_manager.h** - Defines:\n   - opt_pass base class (though it's actually in tree-pass.h)\n   - pass_manager class with pass lists (all_lowering_passes, all_small_ipa_passes, etc.)\n   - Macros for pass registration\n\n4. **gcc/tree-pass.h** - Defines:\n   - opt_pass base class (the base class for all optimization passes)\n   - gimple_opt_pass, rtl_opt_pass, ipa_opt_pass_d, simple_ipa_opt_pass classes\n   - pass_data structure\n   - Macros for pass registration (make_pass_* functions)\n   - Pass execution declaration (execute_pass_list, execute_one_pass, etc.)\n\n5. **gcc/tree-ssa-dce.cc** - Implementation of a concrete GIMPLE optimization pass:\n   - perform_tree_ssa_dce() - main DCE algorithm\n   - pass_data_dce and pass_data_cd_dce - pass metadata structures\n   - pass_dce and pass_cd_dce classes that inherit from gimple_opt_pass, along with their factory functions make_pass_dce() and make_pass_cd_dce(). The registration and instantiation flow starts with passes.def defining the execution sequence, which gets processed by gen-pass-instances.awk to generate pass-instances.def containing member variables for each pass instance in the pass_manager class. Individual pass files like tree-ssa-dce.cc provide the concrete implementations with their pass_data metadata and class definitions, while the pass manager handles instantiation and orchestrates execution through execute_one_pass() and related functions.\n\nWhen a pass runs, execute_one_pass() first checks the gate condition to determine if it should proceed, then invokes the execute method with the current function context, and finally processes any todo items the pass returns. hierarchical registration and execution framework. Passes are organized in a tree structure where passes can have sub-passes, and the system traverses this tree to execute passes in the correct order. The chain involves pass definition, instantiation, and execution phases.\\n\\n## Key Components\\n\\n### 1. Pass Definition and Registration (github.com/sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333/gcc/passes.def)\\nThe master pass definition file defines all optimization passes and their execution order using preprocessor macros:\\n- **NEXT_PASS(pass_name)** - adds a pass to the current list\\n- **INSERT_PASSES_AFTER(list_name)** - starts defining passes for a specific pass list\\n- **PUSH_INSERT_PASSES_WITHIN(superpass)** - begins definition of sub-passes within a superpass\\n- **POP_INSERT_PASSES()** - closes sub-pass definition\\n- **TERMINATE_PASS_LIST(list_name)** - ends a pass list\\n\\nExample pass lists defined:\\n- all_lowering_passes: Initial function lowering passes\\n- all_small_ipa_passes: Small inter-procedural analysis passes\\n- all_regular_ipa_passes: Regular IPA passes\\n- all_late_ipa_passes: Late-stage IPA passes\\n- all_passes: All general optimization passes\\n\\n### 2. Pass Manager Header (github.com/sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333/gcc/pass_manager.h)\\nDefines the pass_manager class which serves as the central pass orchestrator:\\n- Maintains root pointers to each pass list (all_passes, all_lowering_passes, etc.)\\n- Stores an array passes_by_id that maps static pass numbers to opt_pass instances\\n- Contains member variables (m_pass_*_*) generated from pass-instances.def for each pass instance\\n- Provides methods to access specific passes, register dumps, and manage pass execution\\n- Uses pass-instances.def (auto-generated) to define member variables via macros\\n\\n### 3. Pass Infrastructure Header (github.com/sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333/gcc/tree-pass.h)\\nDefines the pass class hierarchy and metadata:\\n\\n**pass_data structure**: Contains metadata for a pass:\\n- type: GIMPLE_PASS, RTL_PASS, SIMPLE_IPA_PASS, or IPA_PASS\\n- name: Pass identifier string\\n- optinfo_flags: Optimization information group flags\\n- tv_id: Timevar identifier for profiling\\n- properties_required: Input properties (PROP_cfg, PROP_ssa, etc.)\\n- properties_provided: Output properties\\n- properties_destroyed: Properties invalidated by this pass\\n- todo_flags_start: Cleanup tasks before pass execution\\n- todo_flags_finish: Cleanup tasks after pass execution\\n\\n**opt_pass class**: Base class for all optimization passes:\\n- Methods:\\n  - gate(function*) - returns true if pass should execute\\n  - execute(function*) - main pass implementation\\n  - clone() - creates a copy of the pass instance\\n  - set_pass_param() - sets pass parameters\\n- Fields:\\n  - sub: pointer to first sub-pass (for hierarchical passes)\\n  - next: pointer to next pass at same level\\n  - static_pass_number: unique pass identifier\\n\\n**Pass type classes**:\\n- gimple_opt_pass: For GIMPLE-level optimization passes\\n- rtl_opt_pass: For register transfer language passes\\n- simple_ipa_opt_pass: For simple inter-procedural passes\\n- ipa_opt_pass_d: For full IPA passes with summary generation/transformation\\n\\nPass registration macros (e.g., make_pass_dce, make_pass_asan) are declared as factory functions.\\n\\n### 4. Pass Manager Implementation (github.com/sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333/gcc/passes.cc)\\nImplements the pass execution engine and instantiation:\\n\\n**Key execution functions**:\\n- **execute_one_pass(opt_pass*)** (lines 2579-2757): Executes a single pass:\\n  1. Publishes before_pass event\\n  2. Calls pass->gate() to determine if pass should run\\n  3. Initializes dump file and timevar\\n  4. Executes pre-pass verification (pass->todo_flags_start)\\n  5. Calls pass->execute() - the main pass logic\\n  6. Executes post-pass cleanup (pass->todo_flags_finish)\\n  7. Publishes after_pass event\\n  8. Returns true if pass succeeded, false if skipped\\n\\n- **execute_pass_list_1(opt_pass*)** (lines 2760-2774): Recursively executes a linear pass list:\\n  1. For each pass in the list:\\n     - Calls execute_one_pass()\\n     - If pass succeeded and has sub-passes, recursively calls execute_pass_list_1(pass->sub)\\n     - Moves to next pass at same level\\n\\n- **execute_pass_list(function*, opt_pass*)** (lines 2777-2786): Public interface that:\\n  1. Dead Code Elimination Pass Example (github.com/sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333/gcc/tree-ssa-dce.cc)\\nConcrete implementation of a GIMPLE optimization pass demonstrating the full pattern:\\n\\n**pass_data_dce structure** (lines 2038-2049): Metadata for the DCE pass:\\n```c\\nconst pass_data pass_data_dce = {\\n  GIMPLE_PASS,                    // type\\n  \\\"dce\\\",                          // name\\n  OPTGROUP_NONE,                  // optinfo_flags\\n  TV_TREE_DCE,                    // tv_id\\n  (PROP_cfg | PROP_ssa),          // properties_required\\n  0,                              // properties_provided\\n  0,                              // properties_destroyed\\n  0,                              // todo_flags_start\\n  0,                              // todo_flags_finish\\n};\\n```\\n\\n**pass_dce_base class** (lines 2051-2079): Base implementation with:\\n- gate(): Checks if flag_tree_dce is set\\n- set_pass_param(): Configures pass parameters (update_address_taken_p, remove_unused_locals_p)\\n- execute_dce(): Wrapper around perform_tree_ssa_dce()\\n\\n**pass_dce class** (lines 2082-2096): Concrete pass with:\\n- Constructor taking gcc::context\\n- clone(): Returns new pass_dce instance (required for pass instances)\\n- execute(): Calls execute_dce with aggressive=false (basic DCE)\\n\\n**pass_cd_dce class** (lines 2121-2135): Control dependence variant:\\n- Similar structure to pass_dce\\n- execute(): Calls execute_dce with aggressive=true (aggressive DCE using control dependencies)\\n\\n**perform_tree_ssa_dce()** (lines 1953-2034): Main algorithm implementation:\\n1. Initializes data structures (tree_dce_init)\\n2. Marks obviously necessary statements\\n3. Propagates necessity through data dependencies\\n4. Eliminates unnecessary statements\\n5. Returns TODO flags for subsequent cleanup (TODO_update_ssa, TODO_cleanup_cfg)\\n\\n**Factory function** (lines 2100-2104): make_pass_dce() creates and returns a new pass_dce instance\\n\\n## Execution Flow Chain\\n\\nThe complete execution chain from compilation driver through pass execution:\\n\\n1. **Compilation Start** (in cgraphunit.cc):\\n   - Calls execute_pass_list(cfun, g->get_passes()->all_passes)\\n\\n2. **Pass List Traversal** (execute_pass_list):\\n   - Calls execute_pass_list_1(pass) to recursively traverse pass tree\\n\\n3. **Pass Tree Recursion** (execute_pass_list_1):\\n   - For each pass:\\n     - Calls execute_one_pass(pass)\\n     - If succeeded and pass->sub exists, recursively calls execute_pass_list_1(pass->sub)\\n     - Moves to next sibling (pass->next)\\n\\n4. **Individual Pass Execution** (execute_one_pass):\\n   - Checks pass->gate(cfun) - determines if pass should run\\n   - Calls pass->execute(cfun) - executes pass logic\\n   - For DCE pass: execute() calls execute_dce(func, aggressive)\\n\\n5. **DCE Algorithm** (perform_tree_ssa_dce):\\n   - Marks statements as necessary based on control/data dependencies\\n   - Propagates necessity through use-def chains\\n   - Eliminates unmarked dead statements\\n   - Returns TODO flags for SSA/CFG updates\\n\\n6. **Pass Cleanup**:\\n   - Executes TODO items (SSA rebuilding, CFG cleanup)\\n   - Publishes pass completion event\\n   - Returns to pass loop for next pass\\n\\n## Pass Instance Generation\\n\\nThe system uses AWK script (gen-pass-instances.awk) to process passes.def and generate pass-instances.def, which defines member variables in pass_manager for each pass instance. This allows:\\n- Multiple instances of the same pass (e.g., pass_copy_prop_1, pass_copy_prop_2, ...)\\n- Automatic tracking of all pass instances\\n- Direct member access to pass instances from pass_manager\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n1. **Visitor Pattern**: Pass classes implement gate() and execute() virtual methods\\n2. **Tree Structure**: Pass hierarchies enable superpass organization (sub-passes nested within parent)\\n3. **Factory Pattern**: make_pass_* functions create pass instances\\n4. **Metadata Separation**: pass_data structure separates static metadata from instance data\\n5. **TODO System**: Passes return TODO flags indicating required post-pass cleanup\\n6. **Property Tracking**: Passes declare properties_required/provided to ensure correct pass ordering\\n\"}"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1701,"cache_read_input_tokens":79216,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1701},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"a6f2cb77-5979-4832-82ff-a3ff61cce2ff","uuid":"9df8d7ef-9b24-4af0-8f29-b70e649feced"}

hierarchical registration and execution framework. Passes are organized in a tree structure where passes can have sub-passes, and the system traverses this tree to execute passes in the correct order. The chain involves pass definition, instantiation, and execution phases.\\n\\n## Key Components\\n\\n### 1. Pass Definition and Registration (github.com/sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333/gcc/passes.def)\\nThe master pass definition file defines all optimization passes and their execution order using preprocessor macros:\\n- **NEXT_PASS(pass_name)** - adds a pass to the current list\\n- **INSERT_PASSES_AFTER(list_name)** - starts defining passes for a specific pass list\\n- **PUSH_INSERT_PASSES_WITHIN(superpass)** - begins definition of sub-passes within a superpass\\n- **POP_INSERT_PASSES()** - closes sub-pass definition\\n- **TERMINATE_PASS_LIST(list_name)** - ends a pass list\\n\\nExample pass lists defined:\\n- all_lowering_passes: Initial function lowering passes\\n- all_small_ipa_passes: Small inter-procedural analysis passes\\n- all_regular_ipa_passes: Regular IPA passes\\n- all_late_ipa_passes: Late-stage IPA passes\\n- all_passes: All general optimization passes\\n\\n### 2. Pass Manager Header (github.com/sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333/gcc/pass_manager.h)\\nDefines the pass_manager class which serves as the central pass orchestrator:\\n- Maintains root pointers to each pass list (all_passes, all_lowering_passes, etc.)\\n- Stores an array passes_by_id that maps static pass numbers to opt_pass instances\\n- Contains member variables (m_pass_*_*) generated from pass-instances.def for each pass instance\\n- Provides methods to access specific passes, register dumps, and manage pass execution\\n- Uses pass-instances.def (auto-generated) to define member variables via macros\\n\\n### 3. Pass Infrastructure Header (github.com/sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333/gcc/tree-pass.h)\\nDefines the pass class hierarchy and metadata:\\n\\n**pass_data structure**: Contains metadata for a pass:\\n- type: GIMPLE_PASS, RTL_PASS, SIMPLE_IPA_PASS, or IPA_PASS\\n- name: Pass identifier string\\n- optinfo_flags: Optimization information group flags\\n- tv_id: Timevar identifier for profiling\\n- properties_required: Input properties (PROP_cfg, PROP_ssa, etc.)\\n- properties_provided: Output properties\\n- properties_destroyed: Properties invalidated by this pass\\n- todo_flags_start: Cleanup tasks before pass execution\\n- todo_flags_finish: Cleanup tasks after pass execution\\n\\n**opt_pass class**: Base class for all optimization passes:\\n- Methods:\\n  - gate(function*) - returns true if pass should execute\\n  - execute(function*) - main pass implementation\\n  - clone() - creates a copy of the pass instance\\n  - set_pass_param() - sets pass parameters\\n- Fields:\\n  - sub: pointer to first sub-pass (for hierarchical passes)\\n  - next: pointer to next pass at same level\\n  - static_pass_number: unique pass identifier\\n\\n**Pass type classes**:\\n- gimple_opt_pass: For GIMPLE-level optimization passes\\n- rtl_opt_pass: For register transfer language passes\\n- simple_ipa_opt_pass: For simple inter-procedural passes\\n- ipa_opt_pass_d: For full IPA passes with summary generation/transformation\\n\\nPass registration macros (e.g., make_pass_dce, make_pass_asan) are declared as factory functions.\\n\\n### 4. Pass Manager Implementation (github.com/sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333/gcc/passes.cc)\\nImplements the pass execution engine and instantiation:\\n\\n**Key execution functions**:\\n- **execute_one_pass(opt_pass*)** (lines 2579-2757): Executes a single pass:\\n  1. Publishes before_pass event\\n  2. Calls pass->gate() to determine if pass should run\\n  3. Initializes dump file and timevar\\n  4. Executes pre-pass verification (pass->todo_flags_start)\\n  5. Calls pass->execute() - the main pass logic\\n  6. Executes post-pass cleanup (pass->todo_flags_finish)\\n  7. Publishes after_pass event\\n  8. Returns true if pass succeeded, false if skipped\\n\\n- **execute_pass_list_1(opt_pass*)** (lines 2760-2774): Recursively executes a linear pass list:\\n  1. For each pass in the list:\\n     - Calls execute_one_pass()\\n     - If pass succeeded and has sub-passes, recursively calls execute_pass_list_1(pass->sub)\\n     - Moves to next pass at same level\\n\\n- **execute_pass_list(function*, opt_pass*)** (lines 2777-2786): Public interface that:\\n  1. Calls execute_pass_list_1() with the pass list\\n  2. Cleans up dominance information after pass list completion\\n\\n- **execute_early_local_passes()** (lines 123-127): Executes early local passes by invoking:\\n  1. execute_pass_list(cfun, m_pass_build_ssa_passes_1->sub)\\n  2. execute_pass_list(cfun, m_pass_local_optimization_passes_1->sub)\\n\\n**Pass implementations**: The file contains implementations of built-in passes including:\\n- pass_build_ssa_passes: Builds SSA form\\n- pass_local_optimization_passes: Runs local optimizations\\n- pass_all_early_optimizations: Early optimization superpass\\n- pass_all_optimizations: Main optimization superpass\\n\\n### 5. Dead Code Elimination Pass Example (github.com/sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333/gcc/tree-ssa-dce.cc)\\nConcrete implementation of a GIMPLE optimization pass demonstrating the full pattern:\\n\\n**pass_data_dce structure** (lines 2038-2049): Metadata for the DCE pass:\\n```c\\nconst pass_data pass_data_dce = {\\n  GIMPLE_PASS,                    // type\\n  \\\"dce\\\",                          // name\\n  OPTGROUP_NONE,                  // optinfo_flags\\n  TV_TREE_DCE,                    // tv_id\\n  (PROP_cfg | PROP_ssa),          // properties_required\\n  0,                              // properties_provided\\n  0,                              // properties_destroyed\\n  0,                              // todo_flags_start\\n  0,                              // todo_flags_finish\\n};\\n```\\n\\n**pass_dce_base class** (lines 2051-2079): Base implementation with:\\n- gate(): Checks if flag_tree_dce is set\\n- set_pass_param(): Configures pass parameters (update_address_taken_p, remove_unused_locals_p)\\n- execute_dce(): Wrapper around perform_tree_ssa_dce()\\n\\n**pass_dce class** (lines 2082-2096): Concrete pass with:\\n- Constructor taking gcc::context\\n- clone(): Returns new pass_dce instance (required for pass instances)\\n- execute(): Calls execute_dce with aggressive=false (basic DCE)\\n\\n**pass_cd_dce class** (lines 2121-2135): Control dependence variant:\\n- Similar structure to pass_dce\\n- execute(): Calls execute_dce with aggressive=true (aggressive DCE using control dependencies)\\n\\n**perform_tree_ssa_dce()** (lines 1953-2034): Main algorithm implementation:\\n1. Initializes data structures (tree_dce_init)\\n2. Marks obviously necessary statements\\n3. Propagates necessity through data dependencies\\n4. Eliminates unnecessary statements\\n5. Returns TODO flags for subsequent cleanup (TODO_update_ssa, TODO_cleanup_cfg)\\n\\n**Factory function** (lines 2100-2104): make_pass_dce() creates and returns a new pass_dce instance\\n\\n## Execution Flow Chain\\n\\nThe complete execution chain from compilation driver through pass execution:\\n\\n1. **Compilation Start** (in cgraphunit.cc):\\n   - Calls execute_pass_list(cfun, g->get_passes()->all_passes)\\n\\n2. **Pass List Traversal** (execute_pass_list):\\n   - Calls execute_pass_list_1(pass) to recursively traverse pass tree\\n\\n3. **Pass Tree Recursion** (execute_pass_list_1):\\n   - For each pass:\\n     - Calls execute_one_pass(pass)\\n     - If succeeded and pass->sub exists, recursively calls execute_pass_list_1(pass->sub)\\n     - Moves to next sibling (pass->next)\\n\\n4. **Individual Pass Execution** (execute_one_pass):\\n   - Checks pass->gate(cfun) - determines if pass should run\\n   - Calls pass->execute(cfun) - executes pass logic\\n   - For DCE pass: execute() calls execute_dce(func, aggressive)\\n\\n5. **DCE Algorithm** (perform_tree_ssa_dce):\\n   - Marks statements as necessary based on control/data dependencies\\n   - Propagates necessity through use-def chains\\n   - Eliminates unmarked dead statements\\n   - Returns TODO flags for SSA/CFG updates\\n\\n6. **Pass Cleanup**:\\n   - Executes TODO items (SSA rebuilding, CFG cleanup)\\n   - Publishes pass completion event\\n   - Returns to pass loop for next pass\\n\\n## Pass Instance Generation\\n\\nThe system uses AWK script (gen-pass-instances.awk) to process passes.def and generate pass-instances.def, which defines member variables in pass_manager for each pass instance. This allows:\\n- Multiple instances of the same pass (e.g., pass_copy_prop_1, pass_copy_prop_2, ...)\\n- Automatic tracking of all pass instances\\n- Direct member access to pass instances from pass_manager\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n1. **Visitor Pattern**: Pass classes implement gate() and execute() virtual methods\\n2. **Tree Structure**: Pass hierarchies enable superpass organization (sub-passes nested within parent)\\n3. **Factory Pattern**: make_pass_* functions create pass instances\\n4. **Metadata Separation**: pass_data structure separates static metadata from instance data\\n5. **TODO System**: Passes return TODO flags indicating required post-pass cleanup\\n6. **Property Tracking**: Passes declare properties_required/provided to ensure correct pass ordering\\n\"}","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
